<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раструб.html>растру́б</a> (21490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trubá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pipe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раструб.html>растру́б</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastrúb</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раструб.html>растру́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раструб.html>растру́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раструб.html>растру́бов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>funnel-shaped extension, e.g. flare <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a skirt, bell, jeans, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, bell <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a trumpet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ochrea, ocrea</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a> (12812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">растяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch <i>(out)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rastjágivatʹ</b> slová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drawl</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rastjágivatʹ</b> udovólʹstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prolong the pleasure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wear out, to strain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">clothes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to strain, to sprain</li>
<li>to stretch out, to spread out</li>
<li>to protract, to prolong, to spin out, to drag out</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растягиваться.html>растя́гиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastjágivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуться.html>растяну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch, to lengthen out</li>
<li>to be worn out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch oneself, to sprawl</li>
<li>to stretch out, to spread</li>
<li>to drag on</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:растянуться.html>растяну́ться</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жка</a> (16944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">растяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastjážka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жек</a></b>)

<ol><li>stretching, extension, lengthening out</li>

<li>device for stretching
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проволочный.html>про́волочная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">próvoločnaja rastjážka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tension wire</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяжка.html>растя́жка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обувь.html>о́буви</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rastjážka dlja óbuvi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shoetree</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pull-action mine, trip-wire mine</li></ol>

***растянуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a> (13301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch <i>(out)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:резинка.html>рези́нку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдвое.html>вдво́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rastjanútʹ</b> rezínku vdvóje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stretch out the rubber to twice its length</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(clothes)</i> to wear out, to strain</li>
<li>to strain, to sprain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:связка.html>свя́зки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rastjanútʹ</b> sebé svjázki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strain/sprain the ligaments</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мышца.html>мы́шцу</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:сухожилие.html>сухожи́лие</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rastjanútʹ</b> mýšcu (suxožílije)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull a muscle [tendon]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stretch out, to spread out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еда.html>еды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rastjanútʹ</b> zapás jedý do koncá nedéli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stretch out one's food until the end of the week</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to protract, to prolong, to spin out, to drag out</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:растягивать.html>растя́гивать</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуться.html>растяну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastjanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растягиваться.html>растя́гиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch, to lengthen out</li>
<li>to be worn out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch oneself, to sprawl</li>
<li>to stretch out, to spread</li>
<li>to drag on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go sprawling, to measure one's length</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растянуть.html>растяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяпа.html>растя́па</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rastjápa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяпа.html>растя́пы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяпа.html>растя́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растяпа.html>растя́п</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gawk, gaper, scatterbrain, <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a distracted, inattentive, clumsy person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***расформировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расформировать.html>расформирова́ть</a> (28653)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формировать.html>формирова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">formirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расформировать.html>расформирова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasformirovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">расформиро́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disband, to dissolve (an organization or group)</li>
<li>to decouple, to uncouple (a train)</li></ol>

***расходиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расходиться.html>расходи́ться</a> (4301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with meaning following the corresponding perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разойтись.html>разойти́сь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razojtísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расходиться.html>расходи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasxodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разойтись.html>разойти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go away, to disperse (in different directions), to spread</li>
<li>to break up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a crowd, meeting, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to part, to separate, to break up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of two or three persons</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to get divorced, to drift apart
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">андре́й <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> ле́на <b>разхо́дятся</b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Andréj i Léna <b>razxódjatsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Andrey and Lena are breaking up.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be sold out (well), to sell well <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a product</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to disagree, to differ <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of opinions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to diverge, to branch off</li>
<li>to miss one another, to fail to meet</li>
<li>to be spent, to go <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of money</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to separate, to not close <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of clothes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:разойтись.html>разойти́сь</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>рас-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ход-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — расхаживаться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>рас-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ход-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расходовать.html>расхо́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasxódovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:израсходовать.html>израсхо́довать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend, to expend</li>
<li>to consume, to use up</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расходовать.html>расхо́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasxódovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расходоваться.html>расхо́доваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasxódovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">израсхо́доваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend, to lay out money</li>
<li>to be used <i>(up)</i>, to be spent/consumed</li>
